Hello,

It seems to me that Wellness Living might know that Yoga Connections has already had a demo and has been paying $99 for months. We were given the impression that we had to "lock in" earlier this year to get this special price and started paying even though we knew that my husband (who takes care of our technology and books) would not have time over tax season to initiate the migration from Mindbody.

I'm really not happy to see this rate still offered in June and realize that we've paid a lot of money for no reason. Also, over the past few months I've seen many concerns and issues brought up on the yoga studio owner Facebook groups about the migration process and poor service and support from your company. 

I love supporting Canadian wherever possible but all of this leaves me with a bad taste and I really don't think I want to make the move any more. 

Not hyped about the hype,
